      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">FIRST
CAUSE OF ACTION</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Claim
for Breach of Fiduciary Duties and Aiding and Abetting</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">65.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Plaintiffs
repeat and reallege each allegation set forth herein.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">66.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The
Individual Defendants, aided and abetted by Longs and CVS, have violated
fiduciary duties of care, loyalty, candor and independence owed under applicable
law to the public </font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
        <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
          <div id="FTR">
            <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
            <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-&#160;16
- - </font>

              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left">
                <div>
                  <hr style="COLOR: black" align="left" noshade size="1" width="100%">
                </div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AMENDED
COMPLAINT FOR BREACH OF FIDUCIARY DUTIES AND AIDING AND
ABETTING</font></div>
            </div>
            <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
              <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="HDR">
            <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">shareholders
of Longs and have acted to put their personal interests ahead of the interests
of Longs&#8217; shareholders.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">67.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Longs
and CVS have knowledge of, and actively participated in, the Individual
Defendants&#8217; breaches of fiduciary duty complained of herein.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">68.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;By
the acts, transactions and courses of conduct alleged herein, defendants,
individually and acting as a part of a common plan, are attempting to advance
their interests at the expense of plaintiffs and other members of the
Class.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">69.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The
Individual Defendants, aided and abetted by Longs and CVS, have violated their
fiduciary duties by negotiating a transaction with CVS without regard to the
fairness of the transaction to Longs&#8217; shareholders.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">70.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;As
demonstrated by the allegations above, the Individual Defendants, aided and
abetted by Longs and CVS, failed to exercise the care required, and breached
their duties of loyalty, good faith, candor and independence owed to the
shareholders of Longs because, among other reasons:</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 81pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;they
ignored or did not protect against the numerous conflicts of interest resulting
from their own interrelationships or connection with the Proposed Buyout;
and</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 81pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;they
are using the proposed sale of the Company to aggrandize their own interests
upon completion of the sale.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">71.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Because
the Individual Defendants dominate and control the business and corporate
affairs of Longs, and are in possession of private corporate information
concerning Longs&#8217; assets, business and future prospects, there exists an
imbalance and disparity of knowledge and economic power between them and the
public shareholders of Longs which makes it inherently unfair for them to pursue
any proposed transaction wherein they will reap disproportionate
benefits.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">72.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;By
reason of the foregoing acts, practices and course of conduct, the Individual
Defendants, aided and abetted by Longs and CVS, have failed to exercise ordinary
care and diligence in the exercise of their fiduciary obligations toward
plaintiffs and the other members of the Class.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">73.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;As
a result of the actions of defendants, plaintiffs and the Class will suffer
irreparable injury as a result of defendants&#8217; self-dealing.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
        <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
          <div id="FTR">
            <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
            <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-&#160;17
- - </font>

              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left">
                <div>
                  <hr style="COLOR: black" align="left" noshade size="1" width="100%">
                </div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AMENDED
COMPLAINT FOR BREACH OF FIDUCIARY DUTIES AND AIDING AND
ABETTING</font></div>
            </div>
            <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
              <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="HDR">
            <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">74.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Unless
enjoined by this Court, the Individual Defendants, aided and abetted by Longs
and CVS, will continue to breach their fiduciary duties owed to plaintiffs and
the Class, and may consummate the Proposed Buyout which will exclude the Class
from its fair share of Longs&#8217; valuable assets and businesses, and/or benefit
them in the unfair manner complained of herein, all to the irreparable harm of
the Class, as aforesaid.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">75.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The
Individual Defendants, aided and abetted by Longs and CVS, are engaging in
self-dealing, are not acting in good faith toward plaintiffs and the other
members of the Class and have breached and are breaching their fiduciary duties
to the members of the Class.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">76.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Unless
the Proposed Buyout is enjoined by the Court, the Individual Defendants, aided
and abetted by Longs and CVS, will continue to breach their fiduciary duties
owed to plaintiffs and the members of the Class, will not engage in arm&#8217;s-length
negotiations on the Proposed Buyout terms, and may consummate the Proposed
Buyout, all to the irreparable harm of the members of the Class.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">77.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Plaintiffs
and the members of the Class have no adequate remedy at law. Only through the
exercise of this Court&#8217;s equitable powers can plaintiffs and the Class be fully
protected from the immediate and irreparable injury which defendants&#8217; actions
threaten to inflict.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">PRAYER
FOR RELIEF</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREFORE,
plaintiffs demand preliminary and permanent injunctive relief in his favor and
in favor of the Class and against defendants as follows:</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">A.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Declaring
that this action is properly maintainable as a class action;</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">B.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Declaring
and decreeing that the Proposed Buyout is in breach of the fiduciary duties of
the defendants and is therefore unlawful and unenforceable;</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">C.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Enjoining
defendants, their agents, counsel, employees and all persons acting in concert
with them from consummating the Proposed Buyout, unless and until the Company
adopts and implements a procedure or process to obtain the highest possible
price for shareholders;</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">D.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Directing
the Individual Defendants to exercise their fiduciary duties to obtain a
transaction which is in the best interests of Longs&#8217; shareholders;</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">E.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Rescinding,
to the extent already implemented, the Proposed Buyout and proposals, voting
agreements and termination fees associated therewith;</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
        <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
          <div id="FTR">
            <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
            <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-&#160;18
- - </font>

              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left">
                <div>
                  <hr style="COLOR: black" align="left" noshade size="1" width="100%">
                </div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AMENDED

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">F.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Awarding
plaintiffs the costs and disbursements of this action, including reasonable
attorneys&#8217; and experts&#8217; fees; and</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">G.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
Granting such other and further equitable relief as this Court may deem just and
proper.</font></div>

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">DECLARATION OF SERVICE BY

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">o</font>&#160;</font>&#160;Mass
      tort (40)</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">&#254;</font>&#160;</font>&#160;Securities
      litigation (28)</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">o</font>&#160;</font>&#160;Environmental/Toxic

      coverage claims arising</font></div>

      the&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">above listed
      provisionally</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">&#160;complex
      case&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">types
      (41)</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">Enforcement
      of Judgment</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">o</font>&#160;&#160;</font>Enforcement

      Civil Complaint</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">o</font>&#160;&#160;</font>RICO(27)</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">o</font>&#160;&#160;</font>Other

      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">above)</font>
      (42)</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">Miscellaneous

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">o</font>&#160;&#160;</font>Partnership

                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">CLASS

                  </div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Case

            <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
            </div>

        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="center">&#160;</div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="center">
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
Louisiana Municipal Police Employees&#8217; Retirement System (&#8220;LAMPERS&#8221; or
&#8220;Plaintiff&#8221;) on behalf of itself and all other similarly situated public
shareholders (the &#8220;Class&#8221;) of Longs Drug Stores Corporation (hereafter, &#8220;Longs&#8221;
or &#8220;the Company&#8221;), by its attorneys, makes the following allegations against
Longs, the members of Longs&#8217; Board of Directors, CVS Caremark Corporation (&#8220;CVS
Caremark&#8221; or &#8220;CVS&#8221;) and Blue MergerSub Corp. (&#8220;Blue MergerSub&#8221;) in support of
Plaintiff&#8217;s claims.</font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">SUMMARY OF THE
ACTION</font></font></div>
          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center">&#160;</div>
          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This
class action, filed on behalf of the public shareholders of Longs, is brought
against the Company, Longs Directors (as defined below) and CVS Caremark to
enjoin an unlawful plan through which CVS Caremark would acquire all shares of
Longs (the &#8220;Proposed Transaction&#8221; or &#8220;Acquisition Proposal&#8221;) without providing
material disclosures, for inadequate consideration and under circumstances
unfair to the Class.</font></div>
          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On August
12, 2008, Longs entered into an agreement to be acquired by CVS Caremark for
approximately $2.9 billion via tender offer. As CVS Caremark Chief Executive
Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;) Tom Ryan made clear in numerous public statements in support of
the Proposed Transaction, Longs&#8217; real estate assets are a key component of the
transaction and a substantial expected benefit to CVS Caremark.&#160;&#160;Ryan
stated publicly that Longs&#8217; real estate assets are worth a conservative estimate
of $1 billion, which CVS Caremark would be able to monetize to its
benefit.</font></div>
          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">3.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">After the
Proposed Transaction was announced and CVS Caremark CEO Ryan made his remarks,
several major shareholders of Longs started to question whether the true value
of Longs&#8217; real estate assets was actually far higher.&#160;&#160;Indeed, one
major Longs investor, Pershing Square Capital Management (&#8220;Pershing Square&#8221;),
reported that it had conducted its own market research and that Longs&#8217; real
estate assets were worth significantly more than $1 billion.</font></div>
          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">4.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Soon
after Pershing Square questioned CVS Caremark&#8217;s publicly-stated estimate of
Longs&#8217; real estate assets, another major Longs shareholder, Advisory Research,
Inc. (&#8220;Advisory Research&#8221;), formally requested through a filing with the United
States Securities and Exchange Commission (&#8220;SEC&#8221;) more information regarding the
Company&#8217;s real estate holdings </font></div>
          <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
            <div id="FTR">
              <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                <div id="FTR">
                  <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                    <div id="FTR">&#160;</div>
                    <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
                      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
                        <div align="center">

                              </tr>
                              <tr>
                                <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">CLASS ACTION
      COMPLAINT </font>

                                  <div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Case
      No.</font></div>
                                </td>
                                <td width="34%">
                                  <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<font size="3">-1-</font></font></div>
                                </td>

          </div>
          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">prior to
voting its shares.&#160;&#160;However, the Chairman of Advisory Research was
told directly by Longs&#8217; CEO Warren Bryant that <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Longs signed an
agreement with CVS Caremark that it would not reveal the value of its real
estate assets.</font>&#160;&#160;In other words, Longs shareholders are being
asked to make the most important, fundamental decision <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8211;</font> whether to
relinquish their shares in exchange for cash <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8211;</font> without the
benefit of necessary material information to which they are
entitled.</font></div>
          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">5.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In
addition, the agreement entered into between Longs, CVS Caremark and Blue
MergerSub erects several barriers meant to deter competing bids and to prevent
Longs shareholders from receiving full value for their shares.&#160;&#160;For
example, even if Longs were to receive a superior bid for the Company, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Longs would be
required to pay CVS Caremark a break-up fee of $115 million, or an astounding
4.5% of the equity value of the Proposed Transaction.</font></font></div>
          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">6.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Moreover,
the Longs Directors structured the Proposed Transaction so that CVS Caremark
need not comply with the usual corporate formalities that go along with the
usual third-party merger.&#160;&#160;Instead, in addition to granting
significant &#8220;deal protections&#8221; in the Proposed Transaction, the Longs Directors
have granted a &#8220;top-up&#8221; option to CVS Caremark that allows CVS Caremark to
complete a &#8220;short form&#8221; merger even it never pays a price sufficient to obtain
90% of the Company&#8217;s outstanding shares.&#160;&#160;The &#8220;top up&#8221; option allows
CVS Caremark to pay the lowest possible price necessary to get the required
66-2/3% of the Company&#8217;s shares, but enjoy the benefits of a short form
merger.&#160;&#160;Inclusion of this provision makes clear the parties&#8217; intent
to avoid applicable shareholder voting protections at the expense of Longs
shareholders.</font></div>
          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">7.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Consequently,
Plaintiff and the other Class members face certain and irreparable harm if the
Proposed Transaction is allowed to proceed, or if Plaintiff and the other Class
members are forced to evaluate the Proposed Transaction without necessary
material information to assess the value of the Acquisition
Proposal.&#160;&#160;As such, Plaintiff, on behalf of itself and the other Class
members, respectfully requests the Court to enjoin the Proposed Transaction, as
Plaintiff and the other Class members have no adequate remedy at
law.</font></div>

                        <div align="center"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">JURISDICTION
AND VENUE</font></div>
                        <div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">8.&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This
Court has jurisdiction over all causes of action asserted herein pursuant to
&#167;&#160;410.10 of the California Code of Civil Procedure and &#167; 2116 of the
California Corporations Code. </font></div>
                        <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">9.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This
Court has jurisdiction over each defendant named herein because each defendant
is either a corporation that does sufficient business in California, or an
individual who has sufficient minimum contacts with California, to render the
exercise of jurisdiction by the California courts permissible under traditional
notions of fair play and substantial justice.&#160;&#160;All of the defendants
conduct business and/or maintain offices in California, and Longs&#8217; headquarters
and its principal place of business is located in Walnut Creek, Contra Costa
County, California.&#160;&#160;Also, many of the Individual Defendants reside in
California.</font></div>
                        <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">10.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Venue is
proper in this Court because a substantial portion of the wrongs complained of
herein, including the defendants&#8217; primary participation in the wrongful acts
detailed herein in violation of their fiduciary duties, occurred in Contra Costa
County, and the defendants have received substantial compensation in Contra
Costa County by doing business here and engaging in numerous activities which
had an effect in this County.&#160;&#160;Venue is also proper in this Court
because many of those affected by defendants&#8217; conduct reside in this County, and
many of the potential witnesses reside or work in this County.</font></div>
                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><br>THE
PARTIES</font></font></div>
                        <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">11.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
Louisiana Municipal Police Employees&#8217; Retirement System is a retirement system
created in 1973 by State of Louisiana enabling legislation for the purpose of
investing and providing retirement allowances and other benefits for the
full-time municipal police officers and employees in the State of Louisiana,
secretaries to chiefs of police, and employees of LAMPERS.&#160;&#160;LAMPERS is
a shareholder of Longs, has been a shareholder of Longs at all material times
alleged in this Complaint, and will continue to be a shareholder through the
pendency of this action.</font></div>
                        <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">12.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Defendant
Longs Drug Stores Corporation (&#8220;Longs&#8221;) is incorporated under the laws of the
State of Maryland, with its principal executive offices located at 141 North
Civic </font>

United States and in Hawaii, with 510 stores as of January 31,

                                    <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">13.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Defendant

prescriptions annually.&#160;&#160;As of December 29, 2007, CVS Caremark
operated 6,245 retail drug stores, which are located in 40 states, including
California, and the District of Columbia.&#160;&#160;CVS Caremark also operates
a Pharmacy Services segment, which provides pharmacy benefit management, mail
order and specialty pharmacy services.</font></div>

                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">22.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Defendants
Bryant, Dashe, Barnes, Metz, Tanoue, Dilsaver and Wagner are referred to herein
as the &#8220;Board&#8221; or &#8220;Longs Directors&#8221; or the &#8220;Individual Defendants.&#8221; Each of the
Longs Directors was a member of Longs&#8217; Board of Directors at all pertinent
times.&#160;&#160;By reason of their positions, the Longs Directors owe
fiduciary duties to Longs and its shareholders, including the obligations of
loyalty, good faith, fair dealing, disclosure, and due care.</font></div>
                                          <div>&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><br>FACTUAL
BACKGROUND</font></font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The Company Suddenly
Announces A Merger With CVS Caremark<br></font></font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">23.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On August
12, 2008, Longs announced, along with CVS Caremark, that CVS Caremark had
agreed, through an indirect wholly owned subsidiary, Blue MergerSub, to acquire
Longs through a tender offer of $71.50 per share.&#160;&#160;This offer amounts
to a total purchase price of $2.9 billion.&#160;&#160;The announcement
highlights the benefits flowing to CVS (the &#8220;Proposed Transaction&#8221; or the
&#8220;Acquisition Proposal&#8221;):</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
addition of Longs&#8217; valuable store locations in Central and Northern California,
Hawaii, and Nevada will provide CVS Caremark with substantial market positions
in these highly attractive, fast growing markets.&#160;&#160;Further, the
acquisition complements CVS Caremark&#8217;s substantial presence in Southern
California and provides a foundation for significant future growth throughout
the nation&#8217;s largest state.&#160;&#160;The transaction also offers CVS Caremark
immediate market leadership in the highly attractive Hawaiian market, where it
currently does not have a presence, as well as high-quality locations in Nevada
and Arizona.</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Significantly,
Longs owns the real estate associated with approximately 200 store locations,
three distribution centers and three office facilities.&#160;&#160;CVS Caremark
has conservatively valued the store locations alone at more than $1
billion</font>. These stores are located in markets where commercial real estate
values are among the highest in the country and prime locations are especially
difficult to acquire. <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">CVS Caremark
intends to unlock the intrinsic value of these locations, as well as the
distribution centers and office facilities, by monetizing a substantial portion
of these assets over time.</font></font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">*&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;*&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;*</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><br>Tom
Ryan, Chairman, President and CEO of CVS Caremark, commented, &#8220;This transaction
provides tremendous benefits to CVS Caremark by accelerating our expansion in
very attractive drugstore markets and strengthening our geographic
reach.&#160;&#160;In fact, Longs has a significant presence in ten non-CVS
markets that are among the top 100 drugstore markets in the country. More than
490 of the stores we are acquiring are located in the Central and Northern
California and Hawaiian markets, where Longs is a leading
player.&#160;&#160;Longs&#8217; store network in these regions is excellent and is one
that would take a decade or more for us to replicate through organic
growth.</font></div>

                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(Emphasis

                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">24.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As made
clear in the announcement, the valuation of Longs&#8217; real estate properties is a
key driver of value in the transaction.</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">25.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Also on
August 12, 2008, the Company filed with the SEC on Form 8-K a copy of the
Agreement and Plan of Merger dated August 12, 2008, between Longs, CVS Caremark
and Blue MergerSub (the &#8220;Agreement and Plan of Merger&#8221;).&#160;&#160;Further, on
August 20, 2008, the Company filed with the SEC on Schedule 14D-9 a
&#8220;Solicitation/Recommendation Statement under Section 14(d)(4) of the Securities
Exchanges Act of 1934&#8221; (the &#8220;Solicitation&#8221;).&#160;&#160;As discussed below, the
Solicitation failed to make adequate disclosures regarding, among other things,
Longs&#8217; real estate assets.</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Specific Concerns From Major
Investors Have Been Ignored</font></font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">26.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Both the
process behind the Proposed Transaction and the disclosed facts regarding the
Company&#8217;s real-estate holdings elicited concerns from large investors in Longs
that the Acquisition Proposal undervalued the Company.</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">27.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
announcement of the Proposed Transaction came mere days after an announcement on
August 5, 2008, that Pershing Square, a well-known shareholder activist hedge
fund run by manager William Ackman (&#8220;Ackman&#8221;), owned 8.8% of the common stock in
Longs.&#160;&#160;According to a <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Financial Times</font> article
titled &#8220;Longs faces pressure from activist,&#8221; dated August 14, 2008, Pershing
Square also owns derivative &#8220;swaps&#8221; that &#8220;puts its actual economic exposure at
23.6 percent.&#8221; According to the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Financial Times</font> article,
Ackman believed that Longs should receive a higher acquisition price than that
offered by CVS Caremark.&#160;&#160;Indeed, Pershing Square had already
conducted market research to evaluate the regulatory implications of a takeover
of Longs by either CVS Caremark or Walgreen.&#160;&#160;According to the
article, &#8220;Pershing [Square] was surprised by how quickly Longs announced a deal
with CVS Caremark in the wake of its </font>

</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">According
to a <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Wall Street

real estate was worth potentially far more than the $1 billion at which CVS
Caremark valued the real-estate holdings.&#160;&#160;The article disclosed that
on August 15, Pershing Square had hired Blackstone Group LP to assist Pershing
Square in raising the Acquisition Proposal price per share.&#160;&#160;According
to the article:</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Pershing
Square ha[d] been approached by a real estate investor that claim[ed] it could
earn more money selling unwanted Longs sites that CVS could on its own,
according to the person familiar with the matter.&#160;&#160;The potential extra
income from such sales could make the assets of Longs more valuable than the
current purchase price would indicate, this person said.</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As noted
in a <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">New York Post</font>
article titled &#8220;Pershing Craves Higher Bid,&#8221; dated August 19, 2008, &#8220;&#8216;It&#8217;s not
clear it was a fully shopped process,&#8217; said a person close to the hedge
fund.&#160;&#160;Two bidders &#8216;is not a robust process.&#8217;&#8221;</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">30.&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Other
large investors soon publicly joined in Pershing Square&#8217;s
concerns.&#160;&#160;On August 20, 2008, in an SEC filing on Schedule 13-D,
Advisory Research, which owned 9.2% of the Company&#8217;s shares, requested
additional information regarding the value of the Company&#8217;s real-estate holdings
prior to voting its shares.&#160;&#160;The Schedule 13-D stated in
part:</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Reporting Persons [Advisory Research] reviewed the proposed tender offer by Blue
MergerSub Corp., an indirect wholly owned subsidiary of CVS Caremark Corporation
(&#8220;CVS Caremark&#8221;), to purchase all outstanding shares of Common Stock of the
Company (the &#8220;Offer&#8221;).</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">To
evaluate the Offering, the Reporting Persons asked the Company for additional
information regarding the assets of the Company, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">specifically with
respect to the valuation of the real estate owned and leased by the
Company.</font></font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As set
forth in the third paragraph of the Joint Press Release issued by the Company
and CVS Caremark, dated August 12, 2008:</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 72pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;Significantly,
Longs owns the real estate associated with approximately 200 store locations,
three distribution centers and three office facilities.&#160;&#160;CVS Caremark
has conservatively valued the store locations alone at more than $1
billion.&#160;&#160;These stores are located in markets where commercial real
estate values are among the highest in the country and prime locations are
especially difficult to acquire.&#160;&#160;CVS Caremark intends to unlock the
intrinsic value of these locations, as well as the distribution centers and
</font></div>

                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As stated
in the Schedule 14D9 filed by the Company on August 18, 2008, in the sixth
bullet point contained under &#8220;Reasons for the Recommendation,&#8221; the Company, in
evaluating the Offer, considered that:</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 72pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;The
Board&#8217;s belief that the Company would not be able to readily liquidate or
monetize its real estate in a manner that would be certain to yield value to the
Company and its shareholders in excess of the Offer consideration and that there
were significant tax implications to doing so.&#8221;</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In light
of these potentially conflicting assertions, and the absence of any substantive
disclosure or analysis regarding the value of the Company&#8217;s owned and leased
real estate, the Reporting Persons believe that additional information is needed
with respect to the valuation of such real estate of the Company.</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Prior to
making any decision to tender in the Offer shares of Common Stock held under
investment management by the Reporting Persons, the Reporting Persons believe
that they should perform additional due diligence regarding the Company and the
Offer to determine whether the Offer is in the best interests of its
clients.</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">31.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">However,
as reported in a <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Dow
Jones</font> article entitled, &#8220;Longs Drug Shareholders Question Value of CVS
Bid,&#8221; dated August 20, 2008, &#8220;[i]n an interview, David Heller, Chairman of
Advisory Research, said Longs Chief Executive Warren Bryant told him in a phone
conversation that <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Longs signed an
agreement with CVS stating it would not reveal the value of its real
estate.&#8221;</font> Indeed, neither Longs nor CVS Caremark disclosed how they
devised their real estate assessment in either regulatory filings or through the
press.</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">32.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">During
the interview with <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Dow
Jones</font>, Heller stated, &#8220;This is outrageous . . . .&#160;&#160;We&#8217;re
certainly entitled to this information.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">This is an issue
of fairness to shareholders</font>. Management needs to get off its lofty
perch.&#8221;&#160;&#160;The same article reported that Thomas Kirchner, who runs the
Pennsylvania Avenue Event-Driven Fund, believed that the purchase of Longs was a
&#8220;cheap way for CVS to grow its store base in California and Hawaii, which have
some of the priciest real estate in the country.&#8221;</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">33.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As noted
above, neither the Company nor CVS Caremark disclosed the method for evaluating
Longs&#8217; real-estate holdings at $1 billion.&#160;&#160;To the contrary, Longs
specifically agreed to withhold this vital information from shareholders,
evidently at CVS Caremark&#8217;s request. Without this information, it is impossible
for shareholders to make an informed decision</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
                                            <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                              <div id="FTR">&#160;</div>
                                              <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
                                                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
                                                  <div align="center">
                                                    <table bgcolor="white" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">

                                                          <td colspan="3" width="33%" style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 1px solid">&#160;</td>
                                                        </tr>
                                                        <tr>
                                                          <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">CLASS ACTION
      COMPLAINT </font>

                                                            <div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt">Case No.</font></div>
                                                          </td>
                                                          <td width="34%">
                                                            <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<font size="3">-9-</font></font></div>
                                                          </td>
                                                          <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
                                                        </tr>

                                            </div>
                                          </div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">regarding
the value of the Company and the value of their shares.&#160;&#160;The agreement
by Longs to deliberately withhold such basic information from shareholders is a
blatant violation of their fiduciary duty of disclosure to their
shareholders.</font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The Solicitation is Vague
and Misleading in Numerous Other Respects</font></font></div>
                                          <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">34.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Besides
omitting material information related to the worth of the Company&#8217;s most basic
asset, its real estate holdings &#8211; the value of which Longs Directors agreed to
withhold from shareholders &#8211; the Solicitation is materially misleading regarding
other information of necessary disclosure to Longs
shareholders.&#160;&#160;Furthermore, the Solicitation is too vague to afford
Longs shareholders the opportunity to evaluate adequately the fairness of the
Acquisition Proposal and the process that led to the Agreement and Plan of
Merger.</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">35.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">For
example, the Solicitation expounds at great length on prior negotiations with a
party identified as &#8220;Party A.&#8221; (Indeed, Plaintiff believes &#8220;Party A&#8221; maybe
Walgreens Co., based on information provided in certain news reports regarding
the Proposed Transaction.) Disclosures regarding the depth and breadth of any
bidding process are important to shareholders when assessing whether to trust
the recommendation of the Longs Directors.</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">36.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
seemingly extensive and detailed discussions in the Solicitation regarding
numerous conversations between &#8220;Party A&#8221; and Longs included the disclosure that
in May 2008, &#8220;Party A&#8221; and Longs entered into a &#8220;joint defense agreement&#8221; and
agreed to engage in due diligence.&#160;&#160;Similarly, the Solicitation
related that in June 2008, CVS Caremark and Longs entered into a confidentiality
agreement before embarking on the due diligence that resulted in the Agreement
and Plan of Merger.</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">37.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
disclosures in the Solicitation imply that both &#8220;Party A&#8221; and CVS Caremark were
treated equally in terms of performing due diligence and preparing bids for
Longs.&#160;&#160;However, the Solicitation remains vague as to whether, in
fact, &#8220;Party A&#8221; actually engaged in due diligence related to the Company&#8217;s
business, financial prospects, and real estate holdings &#8211; as CVS Caremark
eventually did&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8211;</font> or if the due
diligence performed by &#8220;Party A&#8221; related only to the regulatory concerns that
caused negotiations to terminate.</font></div>
                                          <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
                                            <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                              <div id="FTR">&#160;</div>
                                              <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">

                                                  <div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">38.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
extent and nature of the due diligence performed by &#8220;Party A&#8221; is necessary
information to allow Longs shareholders to assess the value of the Acquisition
Proposal. In particular, Longs shareholders need to know if &#8220;Party A&#8221; conducted
due diligence on the value of Longs&#8217; real estate assets.&#160;&#160;As such,
Longs shareholders cannot evaluate the Proposed Transaction adequately until the
Company makes clear to its shareholders whether only one of the interested
bidders was actually fully engaged in the bidding process for Longs.
</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">39.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Further,
the Proxy should make other disclosures, including whether the negotiating
process did indeed accelerate after August 5, when Longs learned about Pershing
Square&#8217;s investment.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">40.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Proxy
should also explain the basis for the Board&#8217;s conclusion that it may not be able
to monetize the Company&#8217;s real estate holdings for full value, which is listed
as a reason supporting the Directors&#8217; recommendation in favor of the Proposed
Transaction.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Provisions in the Agreement
and Plan of Merger Pose Significant Barriers to Longs Directors Fulfilling Their
Fiduciary Duties</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">41.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The terms
of the Agreement and Plan of Merger are meant to deter competing bids and
prevent the Longs Directors from exercising their fiduciary duties to obtain the
best available price for Longs shareholders.&#160;&#160;The defensive provisions
erect barriers to competing offers and function to substantially increase the
likelihood that the Proposed Transaction will be consummated, and cannot be
justified as an appropriate and proportionate response to any reasonable threat
posed to Longs shareholders.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">42.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">$115 Million Termination
Fee</font>: The Agreement and Plan of Merger requires Longs to pay to CVS
Caremark the sum of $115 million in cash if Longs terminates the Agreement and
Plan of Merger (the &#8220;Termination Fee&#8221;).&#160;&#160;This represents an astounding
4.5% of the equity value of the deal, which is excessive and unreasonable under
the circumstances and acts to punish Longs shareholders and the Longs Directors
for simply pursuing more attractive alternatives, while also deterring such
alternatives from emerging.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">43.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Termination Fee is enforceable even if the agreement is terminated as a result
of the Longs Directors&#8217; recommendation in favor of a superior offer for Longs
shares.&#160;&#160;Thus, this </font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
                                                    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                      <div id="FTR">
                                                        <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                          <div id="FTR">
                                                            <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                              <div id="FTR">&#160;</div>
                                                              <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">

                                                                          <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">CLASS ACTION
      COMPLAINT </font>

                                                                            <div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt">Case No.</font></div>
                                                                          </td>
                                                                          <td width="34%">
                                                                            <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160;</font><font size="3">-11-</font></font></div>
