                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">$115
million termination fee deters the Longs Directors from freely and effectively
exercising their fiduciary judgment in the interests of Longs
shareholders.&#160;&#160;Specifically, the Agreement and Plan of Merger
provides:</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(e) <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Termination
Right</font>.&#160;&#160;If, prior to the Acceptance Time, the Board of
Directors shall have made an Adverse Recommendation Change in compliance with
the terms of this Agreement (including Section 7.04(d)), the Company shall have
the right to terminate this Agreement so long as (i) at least 20 Business Days
have elapsed from the date the Company publicly announced such Adverse
Recommendation Change, (ii) at least 20 Business Days have elapsed from the date
the Third Party making such Superior Proposal publicly announced any material
amendment to any of the terms or conditions of such Superior Proposal (it being
understood that any change to the financial terms shall be deemed a material
amendment), (iii) at least 10 Business Days have elapsed from the date of any
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">bona fide</font> increase by
Parent of the Offer Price with a view to satisfying the Minimum Condition and
(iv) the Minimum Condition is not satisfied; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">provided</font> that, simultaneously
with any termination pursuant to this Section 7.04(e), the Company shall pay the
amount due pursuant to Section 12.04(b) in connection with such
termination.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">44.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In turn,
Section 12.04(b) of the Agreement and Plan of Merger (referred to in the
immediately preceding quotation) states, in relevant part:</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(b) <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Termination
Fee</font>.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(i) If
this Agreement is terminated by Parent pursuant to Section 11.01(c)(i) or
Section 11.01(c)(ii) or by the Company pursuant to Section 11.01(d)(ii), then
the Company shall pay to Parent in immediately available funds $115,000,000
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">minus</font> all amounts
reimbursed by the Company pursuant to Section 12.04(c) (the &#8220;Termination Fee&#8221;),
in the case of termination by the Company, simultaneously with such termination
and, in the case of termination by Parent, within one Business Day after such
termination.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(ii) If
(A) this Agreement is terminated by Parent or the Company pursuant to Section
11.01(b)(i), (B) prior to such termination, a <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">bona fide</font> Acquisition
Proposal shall have been publicly announced or otherwise been communicated to
the Board of Directors or the Company&#8217;s stockholders and (C) within 12 months
following the date of such termination, the Company shall have entered into a
definitive agreement with respect to or recommended to its stockholders an
Acquisition Proposal or an Acquisition Proposal shall have been consummated
(<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">provided</font> that, in each
case, for purposes of this clause (C), each reference to &#8220;15%&#8221; in the definition
of Acquisition Proposal shall be deemed to be a reference to &#8220;50%&#8221;), then the
Company shall pay to Parent in immediately available funds, concurrently with
the occurrence of the applicable event described in clause (C), the Termination
Fee.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">45.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;Last
Look&#8221; Provision: The Agreement and Plan of Merger requires Longs to offer CVS
Caremark a &#8220;last look&#8221; &#8211; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">i.e.</font>, should another offer
emerge and the Longs Directors conclude that the other offer is superior to the
Acquisition Proposal, Longs is nonetheless </font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
                                                    <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
                                                      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                        <div id="FTR">
                                                          <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                            <div id="FTR">
                                                              <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                                <div id="FTR">&#160;</div>
                                                                <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
                                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
                                                                    <div align="center">
                                                                      <table bgcolor="white" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
                                                                          <tr>
                                                                            <td colspan="3" width="33%" style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 1px solid">&#160;</td>
                                                                          </tr>
                                                                          <tr>
                                                                            <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">CLASS ACTION
      COMPLAINT </font>

                                                                              <div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt">Case No.</font></div>
                                                                            </td>
                                                                            <td width="34%">
                                                                              <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160;</font><font size="3">-12-</font></font></div>
                                                                            </td>
                                                                            <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
                                                                          </tr>
                                                                      </table>
                                                                      <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
                                                                        <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
                                                                      </div>
                                                                      <div id="HDR">
                                                                        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
                                                                        </div>
                                                                      </div>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                  </div>
                                                                </div>
                                                              </div>
                                                            </div>
                                                          </div>
                                                        </div>
                                                      </div>
                                                    </div>
                                                    <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">required to offer CVS
Caremark the opportunity to make &#8220;within five Business Days after its receipt of
that written notification, an offer that is at least as favorable to the
stockholders of the Company as such Superior Proposal....&#8221; This provision of the
Agreement and Plan of Merger prevents the Longs Directors from the unhindered
exercise of their fiduciary judgment in the best interests of Longs
shareholders.&#160;&#160;Any potential third-party bidders will be loath to
invest the time and resources necessary to pursue a superior bid while knowing
that CVS Caremark retains control of the bidding.&#160;&#160;For the same
reason, the &#8220;last look&#8221; provision prevents the Longs Directors from freely
negotiating the highest possible price that CVS Caremark is willing to
pay.&#160;&#160;Specifically, the Agreement and Plan of Merger
provides:</font></div>
                                                  </div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">&#8220;Last
Look&#8221;</font>.&#160;&#160;Further, the Board of Directors of the Company shall
not make an Adverse Recommendation Change, unless (i) it has received an
Acquisition Proposal that constitutes a Superior Proposal, (ii) the Company
promptly notifies Parent in writing at least five Business Days before taking
that action of its intention to do so, attaching the most current version of the
proposed agreement under which such Superior Proposal is proposed to be
consummated and the identity of the third party making the Acquisition Proposal,
and (iii) Parent does not make, within five Business Days after its receipt of
that written notification, an offer that is at least as favorable to the
stockholders of the Company as such Superior Proposal (it being understood and
agreed that any amendment to the financial terms or other material terms of such
Superior Proposal shall require a new written notification from the Company and
a new five Business Day period under this Section 7.04(d)).</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">46.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
merger agreement also gives strict notice rights to CVS Caremark in the event of
any third-party offer and requires that CVS Caremark receive any materials that
Longs delivers to a third-party bidder.&#160;&#160;Longs cannot terminate the
merger agreement for at least 20 days after providing CVS Caremark this
notice.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">47.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In
effect, this means that even if any third-party bid comes along in the short
time between the announcement of the deal and closing of the tender offer, CVS
Caremark will have the ability to complete its tender offer before Longs can
accept that bid.&#160;&#160;CVS Caremark will also know everything happening in
connection with the third-party competitive bid.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Defendants Structured the
Tender Offer with an Unlawful &#8220;Top-Up Option&#8221;</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">48.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">CVS
Caremark&#8217;s offer is structured as a tender offer in the first instance, with a
merger to follow.&#160;&#160;A tender offer can close in as little as 20
days.&#160;&#160;As such, CVS Caremark has avoided the usual time period
necessary for a shareholder vote to be scheduled and completed.</font></div>
                                                  <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                    <div id="FTR">
                                                      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                        <div id="FTR">
                                                          <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                            <div id="FTR">
                                                              <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                                <div id="FTR">
                                                                  <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                                    <div id="FTR">&#160;</div>
                                                                    <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
                                                                      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
                                                                        <div align="center">
                                                                          <table bgcolor="white" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">

                                                                                <td colspan="3" width="33%" style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 1px solid">&#160;</td>
                                                                              </tr>
                                                                              <tr>
                                                                                <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">CLASS ACTION
      COMPLAINT </font>

                                                                                  <div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt">Case No.</font></div>
                                                                                </td>
                                                                                <td width="34%">
                                                                                  <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<font size="3">-13-</font></font></div>
                                                                                </td>
                                                                                <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>

                                                                </div>

                                                          </div>
                                                        </div>
                                                        <div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">49.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This
typical time period not only allows for competing bidders to emerge&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8211;</font> itself an
important assurance to investors that the price offered is the highest price
available&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8211;</font> but it also gives
shareholders a chance to assess the performance of the board, including the
negotiation of the merger agreement, and to resist the deal if the shareholders
are dissatisfied with the board&#8217;s performance.&#160;&#160;But the Longs
Directors structured the deal so that CVS Caremark need not comply with the
usual corporate formalities that go along with the usual third-party
merger.&#160;&#160;In fact, the Longs Directors neglected to play even a passive
role, where they would step aside so that CVS could make an offer directly to
shareholders and let the market decide the Company&#8217;s
fate.</font></div>
                                                      </div>
                                                    </div>
                                                  </div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">50.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Instead,
in addition to granting significant &#8220;deal protections&#8221; in the merger agreement,
the Longs Directors have granted a &#8220;top-up option&#8221; to CVS Caremark that allows
CVS Caremark to complete a &#8220;short form&#8221; merger even if it never pays a price
sufficient to obtain 90% of the Company&#8217;s outstanding shares.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">51.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The law
treats corporate acquirers very differently when they acquire less than 90% of
the outstanding shares and when they pay a sufficient price to acquire over 90%
of the Company&#8217;s outstanding shares.&#160;&#160;If a controlling shareholder or
a third party pays a sufficiently high price to acquire a 90% stake in a target
corporation, the acquirer is rewarded with the ability to effectuate a &#8220;short
form merger,&#8221; meaning that it need only file a certificate of merger without the
action of any shareholders or the board of the target.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">52.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Here, the
Longs Directors have granted to CVS Caremark a &#8220;top-up option&#8221; that allows CVS
to pay the lowest possible price necessary to get 66-2/3% of the Company&#8217;s
shares, but then enjoy the benefits of a short form merger.&#160;&#160;According
to Section 2.04 of the Merger Agreement, provided CVS Caremark obtains just
66-2/3% of the Company&#8217;s outstanding shares, CVS Caremark is able to exercise an
option that results in Longs issuing brand new shares &#8211; diluting the existing
shareholders&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8211;</font> at a level
sufficient to let CVS Caremark end up with over 90% of the Company&#8217;s outstanding
shares.&#160;&#160;Section 2.04 states, in pertinent part:</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Section
2.04</font>.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Top-Up
Option</font>. (a) Subject to Section 2.04(b) and Section 2.04(c), the Company
grants to Merger Subsidiary an irrevocable option, for so long as this Agreement
has not been terminated pursuant to the provisions hereof (the</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
                                                    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                      <div id="FTR">
                                                        <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                          <div id="FTR">
                                                            <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                              <div id="FTR">
                                                                <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                                  <div id="FTR">&#160;</div>
                                                                  <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
                                                                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
                                                                      <div align="center">
                                                                        <table bgcolor="white" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
                                                                            <tr>
                                                                              <td colspan="3" width="33%" style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 1px solid">&#160;</td>
                                                                            </tr>
                                                                            <tr>
                                                                              <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">CLASS ACTION
      COMPLAINT </font>

                                                                                <div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Case
      No.</font></div>
                                                                              </td>
                                                                              <td width="34%">
                                                                                <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<font size="3">-14-</font></font></div>
                                                                              </td>
                                                                              <td width="33%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
                                                                            </tr>

                                                                  </div>

                                                      </div>
                                                      <div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8220;</font>Top-Up Option<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8221;</font></font>), to purchase from the Company up to
the number of authorized and unissued Shares equal to the number of Shares that,
when added to the number of Shares owned by Merger Subsidiary at the time of
exercise of the Top-Up Option, constitutes one Share more than the number of
Shares (the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8220;</font>Requisite Short-Form Merger Shares<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8221;</font></font>) entitled to cast 90% of all the
votes entitled to be cast by each group or class of shares entitled to vote as a
group or class on the Merger after the issuance of all Shares to be issued upon
exercise of the Top-Up Option, calculated on a fully-diluted basis or, as may be
elected by Parent, on a primary basis at the Effective Time (such Shares to be
issued upon exercise of the Top-Up Option, the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8220;</font>Top-Up Shares<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">&#8221;</font></font>).</font></div>
                                                    </div>
                                                  </div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">53.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
parties also made clear, in Section 2.04(c), their intent for the exercise of
the Top-Up Option to be on the very same day that CVS Caremark gives notice of
its intent to exercise its rights.&#160;&#160;In other words, as soon as it
holds 66-2/3% of the Company&#8217;s shares, CVS Caremark can close the transaction
pursuant to a short form merger, as if it held 90% of the shares.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">54.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Section
9.06 makes clear the parties&#8217; intent to avoid a subsequent shareholder vote if
possible:</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.2; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.2; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Section
9.06</font>.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Merger
Without Meeting of Stockholders</font>.&#160;&#160;If, at any time after the
Acceptance Time, Parent, Merger Subsidiary and any other Subsidiary of Parent
shall collectively own at least the Requisite Short-Form Merger Shares, the
parties shall take all necessary and appropriate action to cause the Merger to
be effected as soon as practicable without a meeting of stockholders of the
Company in accordance with Section 3-106 of Maryland Law.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">55.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
merger agreement also includes in Section 2.04(e) a provision requiring Longs to
take all actions necessary to circumvent any otherwise applicable shareholder
voting protections, including those set forth by the New York Stock
Exchange:</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">[CVS
Caremark] and [Longs] shall use their respective reasonable best efforts to
take, or cause to be taken, all actions and to do, or cause to be done, and
assist and cooperate with each other in doing, all things necessary or desirable
to procure from the NYSE or any other Governmental Authority any necessary
waiver or other exemption from the requirements of NYSE Rule 312 or other
Applicable Law in order to enable the issuance of the Top-Up Shares to occur
without the need to obtain the approval of holders of a majority of the Shares
present and voting at the Company Stockholder Meeting.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">56.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Rule 312
is the New York Stock Exchange rule requiring a shareholder vote for a 20
percent or greater share issuance. In their rush to let this deal close as soon
as possible, Longs and CVS agreed to seek a waiver around this
rule.&#160;&#160;In other words, even if CVS Caremark gets 66-2/3% but does not
get more than 70%, it will still have Longs working at its side to make sure
</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
                                                    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                      <div id="FTR">
                                                        <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                          <div id="FTR">
                                                            <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                              <div id="FTR">
                                                                <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                                                                  <div id="FTR">&#160;</div>

                                                      <div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">the
top-up-option is effectuated and allow CVS Caremark to close the deal before CVS
Caremark is exposed to any risk of competition.</font></div>

ALLEGATIONS</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">57.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
brings this action pursuant to California Code of Civil Procedure &#167; 382,
individually and on behalf of all other stockholders of the Company (except the
defendants herein and any persons, firm, trust, corporation, or other entity
related to or affiliated with them and their successors in interest), who are or
will be threatened with injury arising from defendants&#8217; actions, as more fully
described herein (the &#8220;Class&#8221;).</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">58.&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This
action is properly maintainable as a class action for the following
reasons:</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
                                                    <div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7">
                                                      <div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
                                                        <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%">
                                                            <tr valign="top" style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7;">
                                                              <td align="right" style="WIDTH: 63pt">
                                                                <div style="TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font size="3" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">a)</font></font></div>
                                                              </td>
                                                              <td align="left">
                                                                <div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Class is so
      numerous that joinder of all members is impracticable.&#160;&#160;As of
      August 20, 2008, there were over 34.8 million publicly traded shares of
      Longs.</font></div>
                                                              </td>
                                                            </tr>
                                                            <tr valign="top" style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7;">
                                                              <td align="right" style="WIDTH: 63pt">
                                                                <div style="TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font size="3" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">b)</font></font></font></div>
                                                              </td>
                                                              <td align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;<font size="3" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff is
      committed to prosecuting this action and has retained competent counsel
      experienced in litigation of this nature.&#160;&#160;Plaintiff&#8217;s claims
      are typical of the claims of the other members of the Class and Plaintiff
      has the same interests as the other members of the
      Class.&#160;&#160;Accordingly, Plaintiff is adequately representative of
      the Class and will fairly and adequately protect the interests of the
      Class.</font></font></font></font></font></td>
                                                            </tr>
                                                            <tr valign="top" style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7;">
                                                              <td align="right" style="WIDTH: 63pt">
                                                                <div style="TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font size="3" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">c)</font></font></div>
                                                              </td>
                                                              <td align="left">
                                                                <div>
                                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      prosecution of separate actions by individual members of the <font size="+0">Class </font>would create the risk of inconsistent or varying
      adjudications with respect to individual members of the Class, which would
      establish incompatible standards of conduct for defendants, or
      adjudications with respect to individual members of the Class which would,
      as a practical matter, be dispositive of the interests of the other
      members not parties to the adjudications or substantially impair or impede
      their ability to protect their interests.</font></div>
                                                                </div>
                                                              </td>

                                                              </td>

      defendants take further steps to effectuate the Proposed Acquisition,
      preliminary and final injunctive relief on behalf of the Class as a whole
      will be entirely appropriate because defendants have acted, or refused to
      act, on grounds generally applicable and causing injury to the
      Class.</font></font></font></font></td>

ACTION</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">For Class Claim For Breach
Of Fiduciary Duty</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(Against
The Company and The Individual Defendants)</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font size="+0"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">60.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
repeats and realleges each and every allegation above as if set forth in full
herein.</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">61.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company and the Individual Defendants owe the Class the utmost fiduciary duties
of due care, good faith and loyalty.&#160;&#160;As such, the Individual
Defendants are bound by their fiduciary duties to the Class to employ all
measures necessary to provide the Class with all information material to the
Class members&#8217; decision on whether to accept the Acquisition Proposal or
not.</font></div>

                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">62.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company and the Individual Defendants have breached their fiduciary duties in
the sale of Longs by failing to fully disclose the circumstances and procedures
of the Acquisition Proposal by, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">inter alia</font>, failing to
disclose the method used by the Company and CVS Caremark to value Long&#8217;s real
estate assets as well as the true value of Longs&#8217; real estate
assets.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">63.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company and the Individual Defendants have breached their fiduciary duties by
failing to fully disclose the circumstances and effect of the Agreement and Plan
of Merger.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">64.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company and the Individual Defendants also breached their fiduciary duty by
favoring their own interests over those of Longs
shareholders.&#160;&#160;Furthermore, the Individual Defendants caused the
Company to enter into the Agreement and Plan of Merger in order to perpetuate
their own interests and the interests of CVS Caremark and Blue MergerSub over
the interests of Longs shareholders.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">65.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
and the Class have been harmed by these breaches of fiduciary duty.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">66.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
and the Class have no adequate remedy at law.&#160;&#160;Only through the
exercise of this Court&#8217;s equitable powers can Plaintiff and the Class be fully
protected from the immediate and irreparable injury the actions of the Company
and the Individual Defendants threaten to inflict.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">SECOND CAUSE OF
ACTION</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">For Class Claim For Breach
Of Fiduciary Duty</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(Against
All Defendants)</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">67.&#160;&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
repeats and realleges each and every allegation above as if set forth in full
herein.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">68.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Defendants
owe the Class the fiduciary duties of care, good faith and
loyalty.&#160;&#160;The defendants breached those fiduciary duties by favoring
their own interests over those of Longs shareholders by erecting defensive
measures to protect the inferior Acquisition Proposal.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">69.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Defendants
agreed to the inclusion of, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">inter alia</font>, an unreasonably
high termination fee, and a &#8220;Last Look&#8221; provision that are each unfavorable to
Longs shareholders.&#160;&#160;These provisions were included in the Agreement
and Plan of Merger to deter and erect barriers </font></div>

posed.</font></div>

</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As a
result of defendants&#8217; breaches of fiduciary duty &#8211; in, among other breaches,
erecting these defensive measures in the Agreement and Plan of Merger and in
their treatment of the Acquisition Proposal&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8211;</font> the Class will be
harmed by not receiving the maximum price any bidder is willing to pay for
Longs.&#160;&#160;The defensive measures erected by defendants, and their
interpretations thereof, impose excessive and disproportionate impediments to
any other potential superior alternative.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">71.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
and the Class have been harmed by these breaches of fiduciary duty.</font></div>
                                                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">72.&#160;&#160;
</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Plaintiff
and the Class have no adequate remedy at law.&#160;&#160;Only through the

protected from the immediate and irreparable injury the actions of defendants
threaten to inflict.</font></div>

ACTION</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">For Class Claim For Aiding
And Abetting Breaches of Fiduciary Duty</font></font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(Against
CVS Caremark and Blue MergerSub)</font></div>
                                                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.7; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Longs

</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">CVS

reasonable disclosure of all material information needed to evaluate the terms
of the Acquisition Proposal.</font></div>

Longs Directors for the purpose of advancing their own interests.&#160;&#160;CVS
Caremark and Blue MergerSub will obtain both direct and indirect benefits from
colluding in or aiding and abetting the Individual Defendants&#8217; breaches of
fiduciary duties.&#160;&#160;CVS Caremark and Blue MergerSub will benefit, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">inter alia</font>, from the
acquisition of the Company at an inadequate price if the Proposed Transaction is
consummated.</font></div>

abetting of the Longs Directors&#8217; breaches of fiduciary duty.</font></div>
